### Code Style üé∂
- override linguist's default language detection ([#3100](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/3100))
- format CSE scripts consistently ([#3020](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/3020))
- remove dead code from Windows build script ([#2361](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/2361))
- read without -r will mangle backslashes ([#1790](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1790))
- only call validate if validate bool is true in apiloader ([#1430](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1430))
- shell commands can only exit with status 0-255 ([#1336](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1336))
- don't loop over 'find' output ([#1329](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1329))
- check for unused parameters ([#1323](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1323))
- use 'cmd foo' instead of 'cmd $(echo foo)' ([#1321](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1321))
- don't use `tr` to replace words ([#1316](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1316))
- check exit code directly, not indirectly with $? ([#1256](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1256))
- standardize makefile syntax ([#1266](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1266))
- declare and assign separately to avoid masking return values ([#1241](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1241))
- use single quotes in trapping exit codes ([#1242](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1242))
- bash parameter expansion replaces "echo | sed" ([#1234](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1234))
- remove unneeded 'echo' commands ([#1230](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1230))
- sudo doesn't affect redirects ([#1213](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1213))
- replace unneeded 'cat' commands ([#1202](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1202))
- expressions don't expand in single quotes ([#1201](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1201))
- remove quotes that accidentally unquote ([#1200](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1200))
- don't use shell variables in printf format string ([#1197](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1197))
- use 'grep -c' instead of 'grep|wc' ([#1191](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1191))
- fix suspicious unquoted literal strings ([#1187](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1187))
- use builtin 'command -v' instead of nonstandard 'which' ([#1185](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1185))
- use 'grep -E' instead of deprecated 'egrep' ([#1186](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1186))
- use $(...) shell notation instead of legacy backticks ([#1180](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1180))
- use { cmd1; cmd2 } >> file instead of individual redirects ([#1167](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1167))
- use #!, not just #, for the shebang ([#1170](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1170))
- the shebang must be on the first line ([#1171](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1171))
- use "-n" instead of "! -z" in shell scripts ([#1166](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1166))
- add bash shebangs to scripts ([#1159](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1159))
- remove literal carriage returns and enable parser errors ([#1163](https://github.com/Azure/aks-engine-azurestack/issues/1163))
